***наяривать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наяривать.html>ная́ривать</a> (23103)</h1><br><hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я́</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>ри<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>.

***не.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> (3)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ne</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle_5">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ne</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">negative in full</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> not, no, -n't, without
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>ne</b> znájet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He does not know.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:долететь.html>долете́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>це́ли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ne</b> doletév do céli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">without reaching the target</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гений.html>ге́ний</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>ne</b> génij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is no genius</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лай</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ne</b> délaj étovo!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Don’t do it!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́ва</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ne</b> govorí ni slóva!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">don’t say a word!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Idiomatic negative usage
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a>) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">(mne) <b>ne</b> po sebé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(I) feel sick; (I) feel uncomfortable</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ne</b> raz</i> ― <span class="e-translation">more than once; time and again; repeatedly; many a time</span></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́дел</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja vídel vas <b>ne</b> raz.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I have seen you often.</span></div></dd></dl></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тем</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:менее.html>ме́нее</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tem <b>ne</b> méneje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nevertheless</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">partial negative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> perhaps not, whether ... or not
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:счастье.html>сча́стье</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:счастье.html>сча́стье</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> что́-то <a href = vnd.unilang:похожий.html>похо́жее</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Sčástʹje <b>ne</b> sčástʹje, no štó-to poxóžeje.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Perhaps not happiness, but something very much like it.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хо́чешь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хо́чешь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийтись.html>придётся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Xóčešʹ <b>ne</b> xóčešʹ, a pridjótsja sdélatʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">like it or not, you’ll have to do it.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>will never <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">implying impossibility to do something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jemú étovo <b>ne</b> sdélatʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He will never do it.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">usually not translated, gives affirmative meaning for expression, especially in exclamations</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>лю́бит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быстрый.html>бы́строй</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:езда.html>езды́</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kakój rússkij <b>ne</b> ljúbit býstroj jezdý!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Every Russian likes to drive (a car) fast!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>Кто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>лю́бит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поесть.html>пое́сть</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kto <b>ne</b> ljúbit pojéstʹ!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Everyone likes a good meal!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></span> sometimes appears stressed, e.g. in the past negative of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bytʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, where the forms appear as <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">né byl</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ne bylá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">né bylo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ли</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">né byli</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (i.e. <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></span> is stressed in the masculine singular, the neuter singular and the plural, but not the feminine singular).
</p>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:частица.html>Части́ца</a>; неизменяемое.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-не-</b>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:адекватный.html>адеква́тный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">adɛkvátnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неадекватный.html>неадеква́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neadɛkvátnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>inadequate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неадекватный.html>неадеква́тные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жилищный.html>жили́щные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:условие.html>усло́вия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neadɛkvátnyje</b> žilíščnyje uslóvija</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>inadequate</b> living conditions</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>crazy, out of one's mind, mentally unstable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неадекватный.html>неадеква́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заказчик.html>зака́зчик</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neadɛkvátnyj</b> zakázčik</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>crazy</b> client</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">inadequate</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неподходящий.html>неподходя́щий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nepodxodjáščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">crazy</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ненормальный.html>ненорма́льный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nenormálʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невменяемый.html>невменя́емый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nevmenjájemyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>дек<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:вата.html>ва́т</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-адекватн-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>бла<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>го<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́д</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

***неблагополучие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неблагополучие.html>неблагополу́чие</a> (32075)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неблагополучие.html>неблагополу́чие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neblagopolúčije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неблагополучие.html>неблагополу́чия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неблагополучие.html>неблагополу́чия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неблагополучие.html>неблагополу́чий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>trouble, bad luck</li></ol>

***небо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бо</a> (340)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бо</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nebo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nebo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*nébʰos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cloud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">нёбо</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">njóbo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nébo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́ба</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>небеса́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>небе́с</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sky
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бе</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>nébe</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in the sky</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коптить.html>копти́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бо</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">koptítʹ <b>nébo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to waste one's life (lit. to soot the sky)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>heaven, firmament
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>о́тче</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>наш</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>су́щий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>небеса́х</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ótče naš, súščij na nebesáx!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Our Father, who art in heaven!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бом</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>землёй</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">méždu <b>nébom</b> i zemljój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">between heaven and earth; in an uncertain situation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>земли́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak <b>nébo</b> ot zemlí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">worlds apart</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:седьмой.html>седьмо́м</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бе</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bytʹ na sedʹmóm <b>nébe</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be in seventh heaven</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превозносить.html>превозноси́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>небе́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prevoznosítʹ do nebés</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to praise to the skies; to lavish praise on</span></div> (+ accusative case)</dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́сть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льцем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бо</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">popástʹ pálʹcem v <b>nébo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be wide of the mark</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>air
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:открытый.html>откры́тым</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бом</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pod otkrýtym <b>nébom</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in the open (air); under the open sky</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́ба</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свалиться.html>свали́ться</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>néba</b> svalítʹsja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to appear out of the blue</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:небосвод.html>небосво́д</a> (21084)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́бо</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nébo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>свод</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:небосвод.html>небосво́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nebosvód</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:небосвод.html>небосво́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:небосвод.html>небосво́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:небосвод.html>небосво́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> firmament, the vault of heaven, the dome of the sky</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>бо<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:свод.html>сво́д</a></b>

***небось.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:небось.html>небо́сь</a> (3160)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Contraction of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бояться.html>бо́йся</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne bójsja</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">do not fear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:небось.html>небо́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nebósʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> I suppose, most likely, probably, I dare say
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:небось.html>небо́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снег</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идёт</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U vas tam <b>nebósʹ</b> sneg idjót.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>I suppose</b> it's snowing there at your place.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sure, no fear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:небось.html>небо́сь</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:замерзнуть.html>замёрзнешь</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Nebósʹ</b>, ne zamjórznešʹ!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Don't worry</b>, you won't get frostbite!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***небрежный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:небрежный.html>небре́жный</a> (12458)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">небре́чь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nebréčʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">небрѣщи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nebrěšti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare native <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бережный.html>бе́режный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bérežnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:небрежный.html>небре́жный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nebréžnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)небре́жнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)небре́жней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>careless, negligent, mindless, slipshod</li>
<li>casual, nonchalant, offhand</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>бре́ж<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неважный.html>нева́жный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevážnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неважный.html>нева́жный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevážnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ж<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невдалеке.html>невдалеке́</a> (10696)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>not far off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:невдалеке.html>невдалеке́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>той</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спальня.html>спа́льни</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nevdaleké</b> ot toj spálʹni</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>not far off</b> from that bedroom</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невежа.html>неве́жа</a> (31423)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">невѣжа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevěža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nevěďa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ignorant person lt; ignorance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ne-</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*věďa</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*věděti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невежда.html>неве́жда</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevéžda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невежа.html>неве́жа</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevéža</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невежа.html>неве́жи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невежа.html>неве́жи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невежа.html>неве́ж</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>boor, lout, ill-mannered person</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ве́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ствен<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a[(1)]. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>неве́жественнее.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-невеж-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-еств-енн</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>
